  262. 138. Mathbox for Kunhao Zheng
    1. 138.1. Weighted AM-GM inequality

MetaMath theorems

Number-theoretical functions

Constants


theta

Constants


Lam

Constants


psi

Constants


ppi

Constants


mmu

Constants


sigma

Extend class notation with the first Chebyshev function.

Axiom: ccht


class theta

Extend class notation with the von Mangoldt function.

Axiom: cvma


class Lam

Extend class notation with the second Chebyshev function.

Axiom: cchp


class psi

Extend class notation with the prime-counting function pi.

Axiom: cppi


class ppi

Extend class notation with the Mbius function.

Axiom: cmu


class mmu

Extend class notation with the divisor function.

Axiom: csgm


class sigma

Disjoint


k n p s x

Define the first Chebyshev function, which adds up the logarithms of all primes less than x , see definition in [ApostolNT] p. 75. The symbol used to represent this function is sometimes the variant greek letter theta shown here and sometimes the greek letter psi, ; however, this notation can also refer to the second Chebyshev function, which adds up the logarithms of prime powers instead, see ~ df-chp . See ~ https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chebyshev_function for a discussion of the two functions. (Contributed by Mario Carneiro, 15-Sep-2014.)

Axiom: df-cht


|- theta = ( x e. RR |-> sum_ p e. ( ( 0 [,] x ) i^i Prime ) ( log ` p ) )

Define the von Mangoldt function, which gives the logarithm of the prime at a prime power, and is zero elsewhere, see definition in [ApostolNT] p. 32. (Contributed by Mario Carneiro, 7-Apr-2016.)

Axiom: df-vma


|- Lam = ( x e. NN |-> [_ { p e. Prime | p || x } / s ]_ if ( ( # ` s ) = 1 , ( log ` U. s ) , 0 ) )

Define the second Chebyshev function, which adds up the logarithms of the primes corresponding to the prime powers less than x , see definition in [ApostolNT] p. 75. (Contributed by Mario Carneiro, 7-Apr-2016.)

Axiom: df-chp


|- psi = ( x e. RR |-> sum_ n e. ( 1 ... ( |_ ` x ) ) ( Lam ` n ) )

Define the prime function, which counts the number of primes less than or equal to x , see definition in [ApostolNT] p. 8. (Contributed by Mario Carneiro, 15-Sep-2014.)

Axiom: df-ppi


|- ppi = ( x e. RR |-> ( # ` ( ( 0 [,] x ) i^i Prime ) ) )

Define the Mbius function, which is zero for non-squarefree numbers and is -u 1 or 1 for squarefree numbers according as to the number of prime divisors of the number is even or odd, see definition in [ApostolNT] p. 24. (Contributed by Mario Carneiro, 22-Sep-2014.)

Axiom: df-mu


|- mmu = ( x e. NN |-> if ( E. p e. Prime ( p ^ 2 ) || x , 0 , ( -u 1 ^ ( # ` { p e. Prime | p || x } ) ) ) )

Define the sum of positive divisors function ( x sigma n ) , which is the sum of the xth powers of the positive integer divisors of n, see definition in [ApostolNT] p. 38. For x = 0 , ( x sigma n ) counts the number of divisors of n , i.e. ( 0 sigma n ) is the divisor function, see remark in [ApostolNT] p. 38. (Contributed by Mario Carneiro, 22-Sep-2014.)

Axiom: df-sgm


|- sigma = ( x e. CC , n e. NN |-> sum_ k e. { p e. NN | p || n } ( k ^c x ) )

Disjoint


k x y z A

Disjoint


x y z B

Disjoint


k y z ph

Essential: efnnfsumcl.1


|- ( ph -> A e. Fin )

Essential: efnnfsumcl.2


|- ( ( ph /\ k e. A ) -> B e. RR )

Essential: efnnfsumcl.3


|- ( ( ph /\ k e. A ) -> ( exp ` B ) e. NN )

Finite sum closure in the log-integers. (Contributed by Mario Carneiro, 7-Apr-2016.)

Essential: sqff1o.1


|- S = { x e. NN | ( ( mmu ` x ) =/= 0 /\ x || N ) }

Essential: sqff1o.2


|- F = ( n e. S |-> { p e. Prime | p || n } )

Essential: sqff1o.3


|- G = ( n e. NN |-> ( p e. Prime |-> ( p pCnt n ) ) )

There is a bijection from the squarefree divisors of a number N to the powerset of the prime divisors of N . Among other things, this implies that a number has 2 ^ k squarefree divisors where k is the number of prime divisors, and a squarefree number has 2 ^ k divisors (because all divisors of a squarefree number are squarefree). The inverse function to F takes the product of all the primes in some subset of prime divisors of N . (Contributed by Mario Carneiro, 1-Jul-2015.)

Essential: muinv.1


|- ( ph -> F : NN --> CC )

Essential: muinv.2


|- ( ph -> G = ( n e. NN |-> sum_ k e. { x e. NN | x || n } ( F ` k ) ) )

The Mbius inversion formula. If G ( n ) = sum_ k || n F ( k ) for every n e. NN , then F ( n ) = sum_ k || n mmu ( k ) G ( n / k ) = sum_ k || n mmu ( n / k ) G ( k ) , i.e. the Mbius function is the Dirichlet convolution inverse of the constant function 1 . Theorem 2.9 in [ApostolNT] p. 32. (Contributed by Mario Carneiro, 2-Jul-2015.)

Essential: dvdsmulf1o.z


|- Z = { x e. NN | x || ( M x. N ) }

If M and N are two coprime integers, multiplication forms a bijection from the set of pairs <. j , k >. where j || M and k || N , to the set of divisors of M x. N . (Contributed by Mario Carneiro, 2-Jul-2015.)

Essential: fsumvma.1


|- ( x = ( p ^ k ) -> B = C )

Essential: fsumvma.2


|- ( ph -> A e. Fin )

|- ( ph -> A C_ NN )

Essential: fsumvma.4

Essential: fsumvma.5

Essential: fsumvma.7


|- ( ( ph /\ ( x e. A /\ ( Lam ` x ) = 0 ) ) -> B = 0 )

The logarithmic analogue of ~ pcprod . The sum of the logarithms of the primes dividing A multiplied by their powers yields the logarithm of A . (Contributed by Mario Carneiro, 15-Apr-2016.)

The second Chebyshev function is the sum of the theta function at arguments quickly approaching zero. (This is usually stated as an infinite sum, but after a certain point, the terms are all zero, and it is easier for us to use an explicit finite sum.) (Contributed by Mario Carneiro, 7-Apr-2016.)

Write out ~ logfacrlim as a sum of logs. (Contributed by Mario Carneiro, 18-May-2016.) (Revised by Mario Carneiro, 22-May-2016.)

Theorem: logfacrlim2


|- ( x e. RR+ |-> sum_ n e. ( 1 ... ( |_ ` x ) ) ( ( log ` ( x / n ) ) / x ) ) ~~>r 1
